***фраер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a> (14081)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>There are a number of theories about the origin of this term:
</p>
<ul><li>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Freier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suitor, bachelor; customer of prostitutes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">frei</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First used by prostitutes in Odessa's criminal world to refer to their clients.</li>
<li>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Freiherr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">frei</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Herr</i>.</li>
<li>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">פֿרײַער</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">frayer</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">פֿרײַ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fray</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Referring to someone who has not served time in prison.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">frájer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фраера́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́еры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фраеро́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́еров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> not a criminal person, a potential victim of a crime, any person (male); a person criminals may consider as deserving of respect, even if he doesn't belong to their group.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:устремляться.html>устремля́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I <b>frájer</b> ustremljálsja v stóronu bedý svojéj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And the guy just went towards his trouble</span></dd></dl></div> ("<i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнечный.html>со́лнечной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороне́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a></i>", <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дина.html>Ди́на</a> Рубина</b>)</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вор</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:честный.html>че́стный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne vor, ja čéstnyj <b>frájer</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm not a thief, I'm an honest bloke</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an unpleasant person, e.g. someone who behaves arrogantly, spoils a party, etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жадность.html>жа́дность</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ера</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погубить.html>погу́бит</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Žádnostʹ <b>frájera</b> pogúbit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Greed will kill the bad guy.</span></dd></dl></div> (<i>saying</i>)</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соизволить.html>соизво́лил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позвонить.html>позвони́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хотя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:названивать.html>назва́нивал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:течение.html>тече́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́скольких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot <b>frájer</b> dáže ne soizvólil mne pozvonítʹ, xotjá ja jemú nazvánival v tečénije néskolʹkix dnej.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And this jerk didn't even condescend to call me, although I kept calling him for a few days.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A naive or inexperienced person, a sucker, mug, patsy or sap; one who accedes to all requests, and is easily taken advantage of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дит</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Box ne <b>frájer</b>, on vsjó vídit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">God is not a sucker, he sees everything.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">frant</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rogue, clown, comedian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from a diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">František</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">given name</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:франт.html>франт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">frant</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:франт.html>фра́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:франт.html>фра́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:франт.html>фра́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dandy, fop, beau</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фронт.html>фронт</a> (923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Front</i>.

</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fuge</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">fuga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fuga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***фужер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́р</a> (12763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Late 19th century after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">verre de fougère</i>, a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.lareveillee.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/02/Le-verre-de-foug%C3%A8re-dans-Circulaire-n%C2%B0116-de-d%C3%A9cembre-20151.pdf">certain quality grade</a> of wine glasses, made from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fougère</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ash, manufactered particularly in the town <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">Fougères</i> having its name from abundance in fern and later a glassware industry by reason of this fern presence.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fužér</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tall wine glass</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:функциональный.html>функциона́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">funkcionálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)функциона́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)функциона́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> medicine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> functional

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:функциональный.html>функциона́льное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстройство.html>расстро́йство</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>funkcionálʹnoje</b> rasstrójstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>functional</b> disorder</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***фунт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фунт</a> (6842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pfund</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фунт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">funt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фу́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фу́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фу́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pound (409.51241 grams)</li>
<li>English pound (453.59237 grams)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">numismatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pound</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
